[30;1m34 | [0m[35mHDBSCAN - Hierarchical Density-Based Spatial Clustering of Applications[0m
[30;1m35 | [0m[35mwith Noise. Performs DBSCAN over varying epsilon values and integrates [0m
[30;1m36 | [0m[35mthe result to find a clustering that gives the best stability over epsilon.[0m
[30;1m37 | [0m[35mThis allows HDBSCAN to find clusters of varying densities (unlike DBSCAN),[0m
[30;1m38 | [0m[35mand be more robust to parameter selection.[0m
[30;1m39 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m40 | [0m[35mIn practice this means that HDBSCAN returns a good clustering straight[0m
